Certification and Arbitration
Arbitration
The Institution of Engineers (India) established in 1920 was incorporated under The Royal Charter in 1935 by the then King of England George V. After Independence, the Institution is a “Body Corporate” protected under Article 372 of the Constitution of India.
The Royal Charter has mandated various responsibilities to the Institution, one of them being :-
“To arrange and promote the adoption of equitable forms of contracts and other documents used in engineering and to encourage the settlement of disputes by arbitration and to act as or nominate arbitrators and umpires on such terms and in such cases as may be seem expedient”.
Know More
Register for Certification
Chartered Engineer
Chartered Engineers are Recognized by Peers, Sought After by Employers. Becoming a Chartered Engineer is your definitive way to showcase expertise and rise above the competition. It not only elevates your professional profile, making you irresistible to top employers, but also connects you with industry leaders, opening doors to new insights and opportunities.
Know More
Professional Engineers
IEI PROFESSIONAL ENGINEERS (PE) ELIGIBILITY REQUIREMENT:
Engineers whose qualification is BE / BTech or equivalent, recognized by the Statutory Authority or Government of India and who are having 5 years or more experience, having membership of a recognized professional society and having maintained continuous professional development at satisfactory level, can submit application in the prescribed format to the PE Cell, The Institution of Engineers (India), 8 Gokhale Road, Kolkata-700020.
Know More
International Professional Engineers
A Bridge for Engineer’s Global Mobility
Showcase Your Expertise Internationally through our Int PE(India) Certification
Achieve international standards and regulatory requirements
Know More

Education & CPD
Academic
The academic program of The Institution primarily consists of Sections ‘A & B’ Examinations, widely known as the AMIE Examination.
Section A & B Examination
Recognized by the Government of India, passing the Sections A & B Examination of the Institution is considered equivalent to a degree in engineering in the respective discipline, for candidates enrolled in The Institution of Engineers (India) till 31 May 2013.
Fresh admission/enrollment in Section A & B Examination is put on hold till further notification.
Eligibility Criteria
Section A (Diploma)
Applicable for Senior Technician Members of IEI only.
Section B
Existing Technician and Senior Technician Members of IEI who have completed Section-A or are exempted from Section-A examination, are eligible to appear in Section B Examination of IEI only.
📢 Examination Notice
Summer 2025 Examination-Section A & Section B Grade Card Despatch Details
Eligible students list for Lab & Project for Winter 2025
Apply Online for Winter 2025 Examination
Notification of Winter 2025 Examination
Revaluation of Answer Script - Summer 2025
Publication of Summer 2025 Examinations Results
Roll Number of the Students, appeared in only Project and / or Lab in Summer 2025 examinations
Suspension of Re-Registration / Premature Re-registration
Recognition Status of Section A & B Examination of IEI
Court Status of Recognition of Section A & B Examination of IEI
IEI Accreditation
Accreditation is a formal, independent third-party verification of an academic program or institution, ensuring it meets established quality standards. This process involves continuous assessment, self-evaluation, and peer review, fostering collaboration among educators and industry professionals. IEI accreditation ensures compliance with statutory requirements, strengthens institutional systems, and serves as a preparatory step for NBA (Tier-I) accreditation. It acts as a benchmark for institutions to align with national and global standards in technical education.
History of IEI Accreditation
The Institution began accrediting different engineering disciplines in 1939 with the course of B.Sc (Eng.) at Punjab University. Over time, IEI has accredited over 1,200 courses in 400+ leading institutions, including IITs, NITs, deemed universities, and private engineering colleges. Until the formation of AICTE (1987) and NBA (1994), IEI played a pivotal role in recognizing degree and diploma programs across India.
Why IEI Accreditation?
Accreditation is crucial for quality assurance. With eight decades of experience, a vast network of state/local centers, and over 2.6 lakh corporate members—including esteemed academicians—IEI is uniquely positioned to drive voluntary accreditation. Globally, professional bodies handle engineering program accreditation, making IEI a key player in strengthening India's technical education framework.
IEI Recognitions
MHRD
MHRD has recognized 15 courses of Sections A & B Examinations conducted by The Institution of Engineers (India).
View More
UPSC
The Union Public Service Commission (UPSC) recognizes AMIE qualifications.
View More
Government of India
The Ministry of Education and Social Welfare recognizes Sections A & B as equivalent to a bachelor's degree in engineering.
View More
IIM Ahmedabad
IIM Ahmedabad accepts Sections A & B passed students for its Postgraduate Programme.
View More
IIT Bombay
IIT Bombay accepts Sections A & B passed students for its Postgraduate Programme.
View More
AICTE
AICTE has approved AMIE pass-outs with M.E./M.Tech for teaching assignments.
View More
Engineering Disciplines
Chemical Engineering [CH 404]
Civil Engineering [CV 405]
Computer Science Engineering [CP 406]
Electrical Engineering [EL 407]
Electronics & Communication Engineering [ET 408]
Mechanical Engineering [MC 411]
Material Science & Metallurgical Engineering [MM 412]
Mining Engineering [MN 413]
Production Engineering [PR 414]
Textile Engineering [TX 415]

It acts as a benchmark for institutions to align with national and global standards in technical education.
History of IEI Accreditation
The Institution began accrediting different engineering disciplines in 1939 with the course of B.Sc (Eng.) at Punjab University. Over time, IEI has accredited over 1,200 courses in 400+ leading institutions, including IITs, NITs, deemed universities, and private engineering colleges. Until the formation of AICTE (1987) and NBA (1994), IEI played a pivotal role in recognizing degree and diploma programs across India.
Why IEI Accreditation?
Accreditation is crucial for quality assurance. With eight decades of experience, a vast network of state/local centers, and over 2.6 lakh corporate members—including esteemed academicians—IEI is uniquely positioned to drive voluntary accreditation. Globally, professional bodies handle engineering program accreditation, making IEI a key player in strengthening India's technical education framework.

Education & CPD
Academic
The academic program of The Institution primarily consists of Sections ‘A & B’ Examinations, widely known as the AMIE Examination.
Section A & B Examination
Recognized by the Government of India, passing the Sections A & B Examination of the Institution is considered equivalent to a degree in engineering in the respective discipline, for candidates enrolled in The Institution of Engineers (India) till 31 May 2013.
Fresh admission/enrollment in Section A & B Examination is put on hold till further notification.
Eligibility Criteria
Section A (Diploma)
Applicable for Senior Technician Members of IEI only.
Section B
Existing Technician and Senior Technician Members of IEI who have completed Section-A or are exempted from Section-A examination, are eligible to appear in Section B Examination of IEI only.
📢 Examination Notice
Summer 2025 Examination-Section A & Section B Grade Card Despatch Details
Eligible students list for Lab & Project for Winter 2025
Apply Online for Winter 2025 Examination

Suspension of Re-Registration / Premature Re-registration
Recognition Status of Section A & B Examination of IEI
Court Status of Recognition of Section A & B Examination of IEI
IEI Accreditation
Accreditation is a formal, independent third-party verification of an academic program or institution, ensuring it meets established quality standards. This process involves continuous assessment, self-evaluation, and peer review, fostering collaboration among educators and industry professionals. IEI accreditation ensures compliance with statutory requirements, strengthens institutional systems, and serves as a preparatory step for NBA (Tier-I) accreditation. It acts as a benchmark for institutions to align with national and global standards in technical education.
History of IEI Accreditation
The Institution began accrediting different engineering disciplines in 1939 with the course of B.Sc (Eng.) at Punjab University. Over time, IEI has accredited over 1,200 courses in 400+ leading institutions, including IITs, NITs, deemed universities, and private engineering colleges. Until the formation of AICTE (1987) and NBA (1994), IEI played a pivotal role in recognizing degree and diploma programs across India.
Why IEI Accreditation?
Accreditation is crucial for quality assurance. With eight decades of experience, a vast network of state/local centers, and over 2.6 lakh corporate members—including esteemed academicians—IEI is uniquely positioned to drive voluntary accreditation. Globally, professional bodies handle engineering program accreditation, making IEI a key player in strengthening India's technical education framework.

The Institution began accrediting different engineering disciplines in 1939 with the course of B.Sc (Eng.) at Punjab University. Over time, IEI has accredited over 1,200 courses in 400+ leading institutions, including IITs, NITs, deemed universities, and private engineering colleges. Until the formation of AICTE (1987) and NBA (1994), IEI played a pivotal role in recognizing degree and diploma programs across India.
Why IEI Accreditation?
Accreditation is crucial for quality assurance. With eight decades of experience, a vast network of state/local centers, and over 2.6 lakh corporate members—including esteemed academicians—IEI is uniquely positioned to drive voluntary accreditation. Globally, professional bodies handle engineering program accreditation, making IEI a key player in strengthening India's technical education framework.

GUIDELINES FOR PAPER SUBMISSION
The National Convention is the apex technical activity of an Engineering Division, which is organized annually by the respective Division Board and held on a theme divided into various sub-themes, and hosted by one of the state and local centres of IEI spread all over the country.

Unlock Your Potential
Join our exclusive webinar and learn from the best in the industry.
About the Webinar
The Institution of Engineers (India) is committed towards dissemination of ideas, information and knowledge in the frontier areas of science, engineering and technology through hosting of various technical activities at its various Centres and Fora.
To ensure that such ventures continue to run in a smooth, flexible and ubiquitous manner during this global pandemic time and beyond, the Institution has introduced cloud based event hosting under the nomenclature ‘Centenary Technical Webinar’ powered by National Skill Development Forum of IEI, Shimla. These webinars mark a paradigm shift in the approach of the Institution towards rendering more effective services to its members involving latest digital technologies in the new century.

Education & CPD
Academic
The academic program of The Institution primarily consists of Sections ‘A & B’ Examinations, widely known as the AMIE Examination.
Section A & B Examination
Recognized by the Government of India, passing the Sections A & B Examination of the Institution is considered equivalent to a degree in engineering in the respective discipline, for candidates enrolled in The Institution of Engineers (India) till 31 May 2013.
Fresh admission/enrollment in Section A & B Examination is put on hold till further notification.
Eligibility Criteria
Section A (Diploma)
Applicable for Senior Technician Members of IEI only.
Section B
Existing Technician and Senior Technician Members of IEI who have completed Section-A or are exempted from Section-A examination, are eligible to appear in Section B Examination of IEI only.
📢 Examination Notice
Summer 2025 Examination-Section A & Section B Grade Card Despatch Details
Eligible students list for Lab & Project for Winter 2025
Apply Online for Winter 2025 Examination
Notification of Winter 2025 Examination
Revaluation of Answer Script - Summer 2025
Publication of Summer 2025 Examinations Results
Roll Number of the Students, appeared in only Project and / or Lab in Summer 2025 examinations
Suspension of Re-Registration / Premature Re-registration
Recognition Status of Section A & B Examination of IEI
Court Status of Recognition of Section A & B Examination of IEI
IEI Accreditation
Accreditation is a formal, independent third-party verification of an academic program or institution, ensuring it meets established quality standards. This process involves continuous assessment, self-evaluation, and peer review, fostering collaboration among educators and industry professionals. IEI accreditation ensures compliance with statutory requirements, strengthens institutional systems, and serves as a preparatory step for NBA (Tier-I) accreditation. It acts as a benchmark for institutions to align with national and global standards in technical education.
History of IEI Accreditation
The Institution began accrediting different engineering disciplines in 1939 with the course of B.Sc (Eng.) at Punjab University. Over time, IEI has accredited over 1,200 courses in 400+ leading institutions, including IITs, NITs, deemed universities, and private engineering colleges. Until the formation of AICTE (1987) and NBA (1994), IEI played a pivotal role in recognizing degree and diploma programs across India.
Why IEI Accreditation?
Accreditation is crucial for quality assurance. With eight decades of experience, a vast network of state/local centers, and over 2.6 lakh corporate members—including esteemed academicians—IEI is uniquely positioned to drive voluntary accreditation. Globally, professional bodies handle engineering program accreditation, making IEI a key player in strengthening India's technical education framework.
IEI Recognitions
MHRD
MHRD has recognized 15 courses of Sections A & B Examinations conducted by The Institution of Engineers (India).
View More
UPSC
The Union Public Service Commission (UPSC) recognizes AMIE qualifications.
View More
Government of India
The Ministry of Education and Social Welfare recognizes Sections A & B as equivalent to a bachelor's degree in engineering.
View More
IIM Ahmedabad
IIM Ahmedabad accepts Sections A & B passed students for its Postgraduate Programme.
View More
IIT Bombay
IIT Bombay accepts Sections A & B passed students for its Postgraduate Programme.
View More
AICTE
AICTE has approved AMIE pass-outs with M.E./M.Tech for teaching assignments.
View More

Education & CPD
Academic
The academic program of The Institution primarily consists of Sections ‘A & B’ Examinations, widely known as the AMIE Examination.
Section A & B Examination
Recognized by the Government of India, passing the Sections A & B Examination of the Institution is considered equivalent to a degree in engineering in the respective discipline, for candidates enrolled in The Institution of Engineers (India) till 31 May 2013.
Fresh admission/enrollment in Section A & B Examination is put on hold till further notification.
Eligibility Criteria
Section A (Diploma)
Applicable for Senior Technician Members of IEI only.
Section B
Existing Technician and Senior Technician Members of IEI who have completed Section-A or are exempted from Section-A examination, are eligible to appear in Section B Examination of IEI only.
📢 Examination Notice
Summer 2025 Examination-Section A & Section B Grade Card Despatch Details
Eligible students list for Lab & Project for Winter 2025
Apply Online for Winter 2025 Examination
Notification of Winter 2025 Examination
Revaluation of Answer Script - Summer 2025
Publication of Summer 2025 Examinations Results
Roll Number of the Students, appeared in only Project and / or Lab in Summer 2025 examinations
Suspension of Re-Registration / Premature Re-registration
Recognition Status of Section A & B Examination of IEI
Court Status of Recognition of Section A & B Examination of IEI
IEI Accreditation
Accreditation is a formal, independent third-party verification of an academic program or institution, ensuring it meets established quality standards. This process involves continuous assessment, self-evaluation, and peer review, fostering collaboration among educators and industry professionals. IEI accreditation ensures compliance with statutory requirements, strengthens institutional systems, and serves as a preparatory step for NBA (Tier-I) accreditation. It acts as a benchmark for institutions to align with national and global standards in technical education.
History of IEI Accreditation
The Institution began accrediting different engineering disciplines in 1939 with the course of B.Sc (Eng.) at Punjab University. Over time, IEI has accredited over 1,200 courses in 400+ leading institutions, including IITs, NITs, deemed universities, and private engineering colleges. Until the formation of AICTE (1987) and NBA (1994), IEI played a pivotal role in recognizing degree and diploma programs across India.
Why IEI Accreditation?
Accreditation is crucial for quality assurance. With eight decades of experience, a vast network of state/local centers, and over 2.6 lakh corporate members—including esteemed academicians—IEI is uniquely positioned to drive voluntary accreditation. Globally, professional bodies handle engineering program accreditation, making IEI a key player in strengthening India's technical education framework.

Research Grant-in-Aid
Overview
An exciting opportunity for engineering Students and Researchers eager to contribute to the advancement of technology and innovation in the engineering field—the Research Grant-in-Aid offered by The Institution of Engineers (India) (IEI).
This Research Grant-in-Aid is a significant initiative by IEI, aimed at providing vital financial support and recognition to Corporate Members, Student Members, and Institutional Members, enabling them to pursue research and development (R&D) in engineering and technology.
Designed to empower researchers and organizations, the program offers the necessary resources to explore and develop new ideas, solutions, and technologies. By providing financial backing, IEI ensures that invaluable research projects are supported from concept to implementation, bridging the gap between creative ideas and practical applications.
Key Highlights of the Research Grant-in-Aid by IEI
Financial Support & Recognition
Provides crucial funding and acknowledgment to Corporate Members, Student Members, and Institutional Members for R&D in engineering and technology.
Fostering Innovation
Encourages groundbreaking advancements that contribute to the growth of the engineering profession in India and globally.
Empowering Researchers & Organizations
Offers essential resources to explore new ideas, develop solutions, and drive technological progress.
Bridging Concept to Implementation
Ensures research projects receive financial backing from ideation to execution, eliminating financial barriers.
Shaping the Future of Engineering
Supports projects in sustainability, infrastructure improvements, and technological innovations, driving meaningful progress.
Enhancing Visibility & Credibility
IEI’s endorsement amplifies the impact of research, promoting collaboration within academic and professional communities.
Salient Points of IEI R & D Grant-in-Aid Scheme
Project Category	Institutional Membership	Guide	Student / Applicant Membership	Quantum of Grant (INR)	Project Duration
Undergraduate (UG)	Applicant's Institute should be an Institutional Member	Should be Corporate Member(s) [AMIE / MIE / FIE]	Should be a SMIE	Not exceeding ₹50,000/- for a single project	Not exceeding Nine (09) months
Postgraduate (PG)	Applicant's Institute should be an Institutional Member	Should be Corporate Member(s) [MIE / FIE]	Should be Corporate Member(s) [AMIE / MIE / FIE]	Not exceeding ₹1,00,000/- for a single project	Not exceeding Twelve (12) months
Doctoral (PhD)	Applicant's Institute should be an Institutional Member	Should be Corporate Member(s) [MIE / FIE]	Should be Corporate Member(s) [AMIE / MIE / FIE]	Not exceeding ₹1,50,000/- for a single project	Not exceeding Thirty Six (36) months
How to Apply
Interested candidates may submit their duly completed application in the prescribed format along with supporting documents, in accordance with the guidelines provided.
Deputy Director (Technical)
The Institution of Engineers (India),
8 Gokhale Road, Kolkata - 700020

Research Grant-in-Aid
Overview
An exciting opportunity for engineering Students and Researchers eager to contribute to the advancement of technology and innovation in the engineering field—the Research Grant-in-Aid offered by The Institution of Engineers (India) (IEI).
This Research Grant-in-Aid is a significant initiative by IEI, aimed at providing vital financial support and recognition to Corporate Members, Student Members, and Institutional Members, enabling them to pursue research and development (R&D) in engineering and technology.
Designed to empower researchers and organizations, the program offers the necessary resources to explore and develop new ideas, solutions, and technologies. By providing financial backing, IEI ensures that invaluable research projects are supported from concept to implementation, bridging the gap between creative ideas and practical applications.
Key Highlights of the Research Grant-in-Aid by IEI
Financial Support & Recognition
Provides crucial funding and acknowledgment to Corporate Members, Student Members, and Institutional Members for R&D in engineering and technology.
Fostering Innovation
Encourages groundbreaking advancements that contribute to the growth of the engineering profession in India and globally.
Empowering Researchers & Organizations
Offers essential resources to explore new ideas, develop solutions, and drive technological progress.
Bridging Concept to Implementation
Ensures research projects receive financial backing from ideation to execution, eliminating financial barriers.
Shaping the Future of Engineering
Supports projects in sustainability, infrastructure improvements, and technological innovations, driving meaningful progress.
Enhancing Visibility & Credibility
IEI’s endorsement amplifies the impact of research, promoting collaboration within academic and professional communities.
Salient Points of IEI R & D Grant-in-Aid Scheme
Project Category	Institutional Membership	Guide	Student / Applicant Membership	Quantum of Grant (INR)	Project Duration
Undergraduate (UG)	Applicant's Institute should be an Institutional Member	Should be Corporate Member(s) [AMIE / MIE / FIE]	Should be a SMIE	Not exceeding ₹50,000/- for a single project	Not exceeding Nine (09) months
Postgraduate (PG)	Applicant's Institute should be an Institutional Member	Should be Corporate Member(s) [MIE / FIE]	Should be Corporate Member(s) [AMIE / MIE / FIE]	Not exceeding ₹1,00,000/- for a single project	Not exceeding Twelve (12) months
Doctoral (PhD)	Applicant's Institute should be an Institutional Member	Should be Corporate Member(s) [MIE / FIE]	Should be Corporate Member(s) [AMIE / MIE / FIE]	Not exceeding ₹1,50,000/- for a single project	Not exceeding Thirty Six (36) months
How to Apply
Interested candidates may submit their duly completed application in the prescribed format along with supporting documents, in accordance with the guidelines provided.
Deputy Director (Technical)
The Institution of Engineers (India),
8 Gokhale Road, Kolkata - 700020

Awards and Recognitions
Overview
IEI recognizes the professional excellence of practising engineers, best papers published in IEI Journals, highlights the performance of industry Leaders and academic institutions for nation building.
Industry Excellence Award
The benchmarks created by the industries in India have included productivity, quality, safety and performance assurance thereby giving India the rightful place in the global markets. Realizing that such industries can provide the leadership to a large number of other industries in the country, IEI instituted the IEI Industry Excellence Awards in the year 2008, so as to recognize industry leaders for their innovation, excellence in engineering operations and thereby enable them to lead their industry in a competitive manner. Industries, namely, Tata Consultancy Services, Steel Authority of India Limited, Tata Motors Limited, Larsen & Toubro Limited, Neyveli Lignite Corporation Limited, Bharat Heavy Electricals Limited, National Thermal Power Corporation Limited, Hindustan Aeronautics Limited, J K Tyre and Industries Limited, MECON Limited, NBCC (India) Limited, Goa Shipyard Ltd. are amongst the recipients of the Award.
List Of Recipients
Nomination Form IEA 2026
IEA Brochure 2026
Engineering Education Excellence Award
The IEI Engineering Education Excellence Award has been instituted to recognize leading Engineering Educational Institutions and encourage for better and effective engineering education across the country. Significant development has taken place in the engineering education sector which has created benchmarks for the others to follow. The universities and institutions are no more confined to pedagogy but also diversified to R&D activities , Consultancy, Patents, Publication, Skill Development Programs, Industry interface and introduction of New Education Policy (NEP), thereby giving India the rightful place globally. Realizing that such institution can provide the leadership to a large number of others in the country, it has been considered appropriate by the IEI Council to institute the IEI Engineering Education Excellence Awards.
List Of Recipients
Nomination Form EEEA 2026
EEEA Brochure 2026
IEI Young Engineers Award
With a view to promote the pursuit of excellence in the field of engineering, IEI has instituted 'IEI Young Engineers Award'. The Award consists of a Plaque and a Certificate. The purpose of the Award is to recognize outstanding achievements/contributions made by young engineers in engineering research, excellence in engineering technology development, technology transfer, etc. Any engineer citizen of India not older than 35 years of age/ women engineer citizen not older than 37 years of age as on March 31, 2025 is eligible for the Award, provided that he/she is a Corporate Member of IEI or has applied for IEI Membership. The IEI Young Engineers Award is presented to awardees for all the 15 Engineering Divisions of the IEI during the respective National Conventions.
The awardees attending the National Convention will be provided with free accommodation & their traveling expenses (AC-3 Tier train fare by shortest route) will be reimbursed on production of original documents.
Recipients Of IEI Young Engineers Award
Notification for YEA 2026
YEA Application Form 2026
Prize for Best Papers published in IEI Springer Journals
The Institution gives away a large number of prizes, awards and certificates to the authors of the papers of high technical standard published in the IEI-Springer Journals of all Divisions and thereby extending recognition to individual achievements and activities in advancing the science and the art of engineering.
Best Journal Paper Prizes
The SAIL Awards
To mark the special occasion of the Golden Jubilee of the Institution held in February 1970, the Hindustan Steel Limited (now Steel Authority of India Limited), Ranchi, donated two gold medals, known as the 'Dr M Visvesvaraya Memorial Gold Me
...[truncated]

The purpose of the Award is to recognize outstanding achievements/contributions made by young engineers in engineering research, excellence in engineering technology development, technology transfer, etc. Any engineer citizen of India not older than 35 years of age/ women engineer citizen not older than 37 years of age as on March 31, 2025 is eligible for the Award, provided that he/she is a Corporate Member of IEI or has applied for IEI Membership. The IEI Young Engineers Award is presented to awardees for all the 15 Engineering Divisions of the IEI during the respective National Conventions.
The awardees attending the National Convention will be provided with free accommodation & their traveling expenses (AC-3 Tier train fare by shortest route) will be reimbursed on production of original documents.
Recipients Of IEI Young Engineers Award
Notification for YEA 2026
YEA Application Form 2026

The universities and institutions are no more confined to pedagogy but also diversified to R&D activities , Consultancy, Patents, Publication, Skill Development Programs, Industry interface and introduction of New Education Policy (NEP), thereby giving India the rightful place globally. ======================================================================
PAGE : Technical Activity - National Convention
URL  : https://www.ieindia.org/web/technical-activity#nationalconvention
TITLE: IEI
STATUS: ok | HTTP 200
----------------------------------------------------------------------
CONTENT:
Contact Us
LOGIN
Pull to refresh
Technical Events
National Convention
The National Convention is the apex technical activity of an Engineering Division, which is organized annually by the respective Division Board and held on a theme divided into various sub-themes, and hosted by one of the state and local centres of IEI spread all over the country.
Know More
All India One Day Seminar & workshop
The Institution of Engineers (India) organises a number of Seminars and Workshops as sponsored technical activities, under the aegis of the respective Engineering Division. These Seminars and Workshops are held on various relevant topics related to engineering and hosted by different state and local centres of IEI spread all over the country.
Know More
IEI Technical Webinar
IEI is organizing technical webinars on contemporary topics in engineering and technology in association with industries and academic institutions.
Know More
Statutory Days
The Institution organises, some of the special technical events, to be celebrated on a central theme, as identified by United Nations and other agencies like ITU, BIS and others. These days are known as the statutory days and are observed by all state and local centres and overseas chapters of IEI.
4 MARCH
WORLD ENGINEERING DAY FOR SUSTAINABLE DEVELOPMENT
United Nations Educational Scientific and Cultural Organisation (UNESCO) has proclaimed 4th March as World Engineering Day for Sustainable Development. Engineering is essential for economic advancement and restoration of natural resources. The World Engineering Day provides an opportunity for dialogue between engineers, decision makers, industry leaders, scientists, NGOs and the public at large to address the World's most pressing issues and opens an avenue for presenting the recent achievements of engineers and how engineering and technology are central to modern life and sustainable development.
SMART ENGINEERING FOR A SUSTAINABLE FUTURE [THEME]
World Engineering Day for Sustainable Development 2026
22 MARCH
WORLD WATER DAY
The theme and write-up for the World Water Day which is observed on March 22 every year, are given by United Nations. CATE approved the change in nomenclature from Water Resources Day to World Water Day effective from year 2012 and the same is circulated to all Centres of IEI for observance of the day.
WATER AND GENDER [THEME]
World Water Day 2026
5 APRIL
NATIONAL MARITIME DAY
National Maritime Day is observed as a Statutory Day by IEI on 5th April every year to commemorate the maiden voyage of the first Indian owned commercial vessel SS Loyalty that set sail from Bombay (Mumbai) to London, on 05 April 1919. National Maritime Day commemorates our nation's entry into the international mercantile shipping community in 1919.
MARITIME INDIA-EMPOWERING PROGRESS [THEME]
National Maritime Day 2026
17 MAY
WORLD TELECOMMUNICATION AND INFORMATION SOCIETY DAY
The theme for the World Telecommunication and Information Society Day is obtained from International Telecommunication Union, Geneva, Switzerland and is circulated to all Centres for the observance of the day on May 17 every year.
DIGITAL LIFELINES : STRENGTHENING RESILIENCE IN A CONNECTED WORLD [THEME]
World Telecommunication and Information Society Day 2026
5 JUNE
WORLD ENVIRONMENT DAY
The theme for the World Environment Day is obtained from the HQrs of UNEP and is circulated to all Centres for the observance of the day on June 5 every year.
A GLOBAL CALL FOR CLIMATE ACTION [THEME]
World Environment Day 2026
9 SEPTEMBER
ROYAL CHARTER DAY
Established in 1920, with its headquarters at 8 Gokhale Road, Kolkata-700020, The Institution of Engineers (India) was incorporated by Royal Charter on September 09, 1935 and remains the only professional body in India to be accorded this honour.
September 09 of every year, is observed as Royal Charter Day by all Centres of IEI. On this auspicious day, Royal Charter of Incorporation was granted to IEI by His Majesty, The King and Emperor George
...[truncated]

LOGIN
Pull to refresh
Technical Events
National Convention
The National Convention is the apex technical activity of an Engineering Division, which is organized annually by the respective Division Board and held on a theme divided into various sub-themes, and hosted by one of the state and local centres of IEI spread all over the country.
Know More
All India One Day Seminar & workshop
The Institution of Engineers (India) organises a number of Seminars and Workshops as sponsored technical activities, under the aegis of the respective Engineering Division. These Seminars and Workshops are held on various relevant topics related to engineering and hosted by different state and local centres of IEI spread all over the country.
Know More
IEI Technical Webinar
IEI is organizing technical webinars on contemporary topics in engineering and technology in association with industries and academic institutions.
Know More
Statutory Days
The Institution organises, some of the special technical events, to be celebrated on a central theme, as identified by United Nations and other agencies like ITU, BIS and others. These days are known as the statutory days and are observed by all state and local centres and overseas chapters of IEI.
4 MARCH
WORLD ENGINEERING DAY FOR SUSTAINABLE DEVELOPMENT
United Nations Educational Scientific and Cultural Organisation (UNESCO) has proclaimed 4th March as World Engineering Day for Sustainable Development. Engineering is essential for economic advancement and restoration of natural resources. The World Engineering Day provides an opportunity for dialogue between engineers, decision makers, industry leaders, scientists, NGOs and the public at large to address the World's most pressing issues and opens an avenue for presenting the recent achievements of engineers and how engineering and technology are central to modern life and sustainable development.
SMART ENGINEERING FOR A SUSTAINABLE FUTURE [THEME]
World Engineering Day for Sustainable Development 2026
22 MARCH
WORLD WATER DAY
The theme and write-up for the World Water Day which is observed on March 22 every year, are given by United Nations. CATE approved the change in nomenclature from Water Resources Day to World Water Day effective from year 2012 and the same is circulated to all Centres of IEI for observance of the day.
WATER AND GENDER [THEME]
World Water Day 2026
5 APRIL
NATIONAL MARITIME DAY
National Maritime Day is observed as a Statutory Day by IEI on 5th April every year to commemorate the maiden voyage of the first Indian owned commercial vessel SS Loyalty that set sail from Bombay (Mumbai) to London, on 05 April 1919. National Maritime Day commemorates our nation's entry into the international mercantile shipping community in 1919.
MARITIME INDIA-EMPOWERING PROGRESS [THEME]
National Maritime Day 2026
17 MAY
WORLD TELECOMMUNICATION AND INFORMATION SOCIETY DAY
The theme for the World Telecommunication and Information Society Day is obtained from International Telecommunication Union, Geneva, Switzerland and is circulated to all Centres for the observance of the day on May 17 every year.
DIGITAL LIFELINES : STRENGTHENING RESILIENCE IN A CONNECTED WORLD [THEME]
World Telecommunication and Information Society Day 2026
5 JUNE
WORLD ENVIRONMENT DAY
The theme for the World Environment Day is obtained from the HQrs of UNEP and is circulated to all Centres for the observance of the day on June 5 every year.
A GLOBAL CALL FOR CLIMATE ACTION [THEME]
World Environment Day 2026
9 SEPTEMBER
ROYAL CHARTER DAY
Established in 1920, with its headquarters at 8 Gokhale Road, Kolkata-700020, The Institution of Engineers (India) was incorporated by Royal Charter on September 09, 1935 and remains the only professional body in India to be accorded this honour.
September 09 of every year, is observed as Royal Charter Day by all Centres of IEI. On this auspicious day, Royal Charter of Incorporation was granted to IEI by His Majesty, The King and Emperor George
...[truncated]

PAGE : Publication - Annual Reports
URL  : https://www.ieindia.org/web/publication#annualreports
TITLE: IEI
STATUS: ok | HTTP 200

CONTENT:
Contact Us
LOGIN
Pull to refresh
IEI Publications
Overview
IEI is instrumental in publishing journals, books, Annual Technical Volumes, Compendium on R & D Projects, Annual Reports, Proceedings of Indian Engineering Congress, National Conventions, and International Conferences.
IEI Springer Journals
To augment the quality of the Journals, in a landmark achievement, the Institution has signed the co-publishing agreement with M/s Springer (India) Pvt Ltd, New Delhi, on 10th August 2011 at Headquarters in Kolkata. Both IE(I) and Springer have agreed for the common cause of improvement in the quality of journals, impact factor, citation index and also to bring the Journals within the reach of one and all in all corners of the globe.
All 15 engineering divisional journals have been grouped into five series –Series A, Series B, Series C, Series D & Series E.
SERIES-A
SERIES-B
SERIES-C
SERIES-D
SERIES-E
JOURNAL OF THE INSTITUTION OF ENGINEERS: SERIES A
Areas Covered:
Civil Engineering
Architectural Engineering
Environmental Engineering
Agricultural Engineering
Series A serves the national and international engineering community through dissemination of scientific knowledge on practical engineering and design methodologies pertaining to Civil, Architectural, Environmental and Agricultural engineering. Original manuscripts are published through Double-Blind Peer Review in all the areas including (but not limited to) structural designs, green buildings, environmental pollutions or agricultural machinery / techniques related researches. It covers all possible areas of latest research and developmental works in the field of infrastructure developments, waste management techniques, harvestings methodologies, rainwater harvestings etc. so that the researchers, scientists or professionals can easily motivate themselves to pursue the work.
Months of Publication:
March
June
September
December

IEI News
IEI News is a four colour monthly tabloid containing reports of various technical activities of IEI organised by its Centres nationwide under the aegis of Engineering Division Boards and Committees, by the Fora,Organ and Overseas chapters. It also contain the details of forthcoming programmes of technical activities along with other announcements.

IEI Publications
Overview
IEI is instrumental in publishing journals, books, Annual Technical Volumes, Compendium on R & D Projects, Annual Reports, Proceedings of Indian Engineering Congress, National Conventions, and International Conferences.
IEI Springer Journals
To augment the quality of the Journals, in a landmark achievement, the Institution has signed the co-publishing agreement with M/s Springer (India) Pvt Ltd, New Delhi, on 10th August 2011 at Headquarters in Kolkata. Both IE(I) and Springer have agreed for the common cause of improvement in the quality of journals, impact factor, citation index and also to bring the Journals within the reach of one and all in all corners of the globe.
All 15 engineering divisional journals have been grouped into five series –Series A, Series B, Series C, Series D & Series E.
SERIES-A
SERIES-B
SERIES-C
SERIES-D
SERIES-E
JOURNAL OF THE INSTITUTION OF ENGINEERS: SERIES A
Areas Covered:
Civil Engineering
Architectural Engineering
Environmental Engineering
Agricultural Engineering
Series A serves the national and international engineering community through dissemination of scientific knowledge on practical engineering and design methodologies pertaining to Civil, Architectural, Environmental and Agricultural engineering. Original manuscripts are published through Double-Blind Peer Review in all the areas including (but not limited to) structural designs, green buildings, environmental pollutions or agricultural machinery / techniques related researches. It covers all possible areas of latest research and developmental works in the field of infrastructure developments, waste management techniques, harvestings methodologies, rainwater harvestings etc. so that the researchers, scientists or professionals can easily motivate themselves to pursue the work.
Months of Publication:
March
June
September
December

IEI Publications
Overview
IEI is instrumental in publishing journals, books, Annual Technical Volumes, Compendium on R & D Projects, Annual Reports, Proceedings of Indian Engineering Congress, National Conventions, and International Conferences.
IEI Springer Journals
To augment the quality of the Journals, in a landmark achievement, the Institution has signed the co-publishing agreement with M/s Springer (India) Pvt Ltd, New Delhi, on 10th August 2011 at Headquarters in Kolkata. Both IE(I) and Springer have agreed for the common cause of improvement in the quality of journals, impact factor, citation index and also to bring the Journals within the reach of one and all in all corners of the globe.
All 15 engineering divisional journals have been grouped into five series –Series A, Series B, Series C, Series D & Series E.
SERIES-A
SERIES-B
SERIES-C
SERIES-D
SERIES-E
JOURNAL OF THE INSTITUTION OF ENGINEERS: SERIES A
Areas Covered:
Civil Engineering
Architectural Engineering
Environmental Engineering
Agricultural Engineering
Series A serves the national and international engineering community through dissemination of scientific knowledge on practical engineering and design methodologies pertaining to Civil, Architectural, Environmental and Agricultural engineering. Original manuscripts are published through Double-Blind Peer Review in all the areas including (but not limited to) structural designs, green buildings, environmental pollutions or agricultural machinery / techniques related researches. It covers all possible areas of latest research and developmental works in the field of infrastructure developments, waste management techniques, harvestings methodologies, rainwater harvestings etc. so that the researchers, scientists or professionals can easily motivate themselves to pursue the work.
Months of Publication:
March
June
September
December

IEI News
IEI News is a four colour monthly tabloid containing reports of various technical activities of IEI organised by its Centres nationwide under the aegis of Engineering Division Boards and Committees, by the Fora,Organ and Overseas chapters. It also contain the details of forthcoming programmes of technical activities along with other announcements.

IEI Epitom is a monthly e-Newsletter dedicated to the Corporate and Institutional Members of the august body where they can share their achievements, Success Stories, Publications etc.

Annual Technical Volume
Annual Technical Volume is published by the respective Engineering Division Board and Interdisciplinary Coordination Committee based on invited papers from eminent engineers on contemporary issues having technical relevance. Papers/Lectures presented in National Convention and in All India Seminars are also given priority.

Certification and Arbitration
Arbitration
The Institution of Engineers (India) established in 1920 was incorporated under The Royal Charter in 1935 by the then King of England George V. After Independence, the Institution is a “Body Corporate” protected under Article 372 of the Constitution of India.
The Royal Charter has mandated various responsibilities to the Institution, one of them being :-
“To arrange and promote the adoption of equitable forms of contracts and other documents used in engineering and to encourage the settlement of disputes by arbitration and to act as or nominate arbitrators and umpires on such terms and in such cases as may be seem expedient”.
Know More
Register for Certification
Chartered Engineer
Chartered Engineers are Recognized by Peers, Sought After by Employers. Becoming a Chartered Engineer is your definitive way to showcase expertise and rise above the competition. It not only elevates your professional profile, making you irresistible to top employers, but also connects you with industry leaders, opening doors to new insights and opportunities.
Know More
Professional Engineers
IEI PROFESSIONAL ENGINEERS (PE) ELIGIBILITY REQUIREMENT:
Engineers whose qualification is BE / BTech or equivalent, recognized by the Statutory Authority or Government of India and who are having 5 years or more experience, having membership of a recognized professional society and having maintained continuous professional development at satisfactory level, can submit application in the prescribed format to the PE Cell, The Institution of Engineers (India), 8 Gokhale Road, Kolkata-700020.
Know More
International Professional Engineers
A Bridge for Engineer’s Global Mobility
Showcase Your Expertise Internationally through our Int PE(India) Certification
Achieve international standards and regulatory requirements
Know More

Become a Member
OVERVIEW
STUDENT
EARLY-CAREER
MID-CAREER
VETERAN
Why join IEI?
Engineering Career Progression - A way Forward
Joining as Member of IEI offers the comprehensive benefits for advancing the professional knowledge and career trajectory. Develop into the advantages and exclusive opportunities afforded to members, designed to support and elevate the professional development.
Registration
Registration certifies the engineering qualifications, ensuring industry standards and authorized to practice professionally.
Recognition
Including IEI post-nominals in your signature and resume highlights your professional affiliation, credibility, and commitment to engineering excellence.
Networking
Join the IEI network for knowledge sharing, collaboration, and staying updated on industry advancements and best practices.
Knowledge Resource
Access Network of IEI-Bibliotheca to enhance professional knowledge and career development.
Publication
Offering exclusive access to IEI’s prestigious publications and Springer Nature journals, valuable insights of research to advance the engineering expertise.
Career Advancement
Several Continuous Professional Development (CPD) program organized by various Forum of IEI and ESCI at Hyderabad to foster the career growth.
IEI: Beyond Membership, Empowering Professionals
IEI provides tools and opportunities to enhance and advance professional growth through Membership.
Choosing Grades of Membership
Wherever you are in the professional journey, Membership will give to you.
Fellow
Highest grade of IEI Corporate Membership, prestigious identity.
Age: 40 Years
Qualification: BE/B.Tech/ME/MTech or IEI Exam
Experience: 15 Years post‑qualification with high responsibility.
Apply Now
Member
Senior grade of IEI Corporate Membership – eligible to use “MIE”.
Age: 30 Years
Qualification: BE/B.Tech/ME/MTech or IEI Exam
Experience: 8 Years (employed) / 10 Years (self‑employed).
Apply Now
Associate Member
Initial grade of IEI Corporate Membership – eligible to use “AMIE”.
Age: 21 Years
Qualification: BE/B.Tech/ME/MTech or IEI Exam
Apply Now
Student Member
For students pursuing BE/B.Tech (AICTE/UGC‑approved).
Qualification: Pursuing BE/B.Tech (recognised institution).
Benefit: Professional recognition, career development.
Apply Now
Member Technologist
Senior grade for technologists in responsible roles.
Age: 32 Years
Qualification: Diploma/B.Sc (PCM) + relevant PG degree.
Experience: 10 Years in engineering/industry.
Download Application
Associate Member Technologist
Entry‑level technologist membership with responsible roles.
Age: 26 Years
Qualification: Diploma/B.Sc (PCM) + relevant PG degree.
Experience: 5 Years in engineering/industry.
Download Application

INSTITUTIONAL MEMBER
Recognition of Organization through IEI
IEI Institutional Members are prominent organizations dedicated to the professional growth of their employees. With over 700 Institutional Members both are academic and industry level, we supported by IEI in advancing their engineers' professional development.
SOME OF OUR VALUED INSTITUTIONAL MEMBERS [ 700 + Members ]
IM0001912
DIRECTOR GENERAL NAVAL PROJECTS, MUMBAI
IM0005748
INDIAN INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY, KANPUR
IM0000075
SURVEY OF INDIA
IM0006132
DELHI METRO RAIL CORP LTD
IM0004458
TATA IRON & STEEL CO LTD
IM0005462
INSTITUTION OF MILITARY ENGINEERS
IM0004415
HINDUSTAN AERONAUTICS LTD
IM0001734
DR C V RAMAN UNIVERSITY
List Of IM Members
Benefits of Institutional Member
Free e-Access to Renowned Journals
Free e-access of all published articles in Springer Nature Journals through www.ieindia.org
Technical Collaboration
Offering technical collaboration and sponsorship for arranging events.
Opportunity for research grant
Offering research grant for UG/PG/ P.hd scholars
Access Library
Accessing IEI libraries in Pan-India basis.
Participation of Seminars
Participation of Deputed Staff (both Engineering and Managerial) in technical events at a concessional rate to regular Corporate Members.
Professional usage of Institution Premises
Use of Premises of IEI Centres for organising Technical / Academic events.
Access Guest House
Facility to access of IEI guest houses to Managerial / Technical Staff deputed by Institutional Member.
Eligibility
Any Public or Local Body, Registered Company or Firm, or an individual may desire to be attached, to IEI as Institutional Member for life time.
Fee Applicable
The fees for applicants are as follows:
INSTITUTIONAL MEMBERS(IM) = 2,95,000.00 (GST included)

Membership
Membership
Upholds Integrity, Excellence & Accountability
The Institution of Engineers (India) (IEI) is the largest multidisciplinary professional body of engineers in the country, fostering innovation, technical excellence, and leadership.
IEI offers prestigious memberships, including Student, Associate, Member, and Fellow grades, empowering engineers with global recognition, networking opportunities, and career growth. Members gain access to seminars, research, publications, and skill-enhancing programs.
With over a century of legacy, IEI membership is a gateway to excellence, enabling engineers to shape the future and contribute to nation-building. Join IEI today and be a part of India’s engineering revolution!

FOR ONLINE APPLICATION THROUGH IEI WEBSITE
Sl. No.	Application Type	Fee for India (INR)
(Including GST)	Fee for Other Countries
(INR Remittance)
1	ENROLLMENT OF ASSOCIATE MEMB. TECHNOLOGIST	3481 INR	28500 INR
2	ENROLLMENT OF ASSOCIATE MEMBER	7080 INR	54375 INR
3	ENROLLMENT OF FELLOW	24780 INR	105000 INR
4	ENROLLMENT OF MEMBER	12980 INR	98250 INR
5	ENROLLMENT OF MEMBER TECHNOLOGIST	4012 INR	33000 INR
6	ENROLLMENT OF STUDENT MEMBER	1499.78 INR	11250 INR
For HARD COPY Applications
An additional handling charge (Rs 200/- + GST) is required as mentioned in the Hard copy application forms.
Application, complete in all respect is to be sent to The Membership Department, The Institution of Engineers (India), 8, Gokhale Road, Kolkata-700020 along with requisite fee in form of Demand Draft/ Cheque drawn on any scheduled bank in favour of “The Institution of Engineers (India)” payable at Kolkata.
For further information email at membership@ieindia.org

PAGE : Student Chapters - Schapter

TITLE: IEI
STATUS: ok | HTTP 200

CONTENT:
Contact Us
LOGIN
Pull to refresh
Student Chapter
Overview
Students’ Chapters of IEI in Engineering Colleges or Polytechnic may be established as per Rules and Regulations of IEI.
The Student Members (SMIE) of IEI shall be Member of Students' Chapters.
Benefits of Students’ Chapters
Unlock endless opportunities for learning, networking, and career growth for Students.
Participate in Technical Events
Seminars, Workshops, and National Conventions etc. organized by IEI State/Local Centres.
Hosting Technical Events
Students can organize various technical programm, Paper Presentation, Model Presentation, Start up Programm etc.
Library Access
Enjoy unlimited access to the IEI State/Local Centre libraries for research and study.
Networking & Mentorship
Connect with IEI members and industry professionals for career guidance.
Exclusive Membership Benefits
Eligible students can become Corporate Member of IEI after completion of graduation.
Scholarships & Awards
Top-performing students’ chapters receive cash prizes.
Students’ Chapter Newsletter
Stay updated with the latest news and developments through the exclusive newsletter.
Publish Research Papers
Students can publish research articles in Students’ Journal released every December.
How to Open Students' Chapters
Initial request from an Engineering College/ Polytechnic to be made to the Deputy Director (Membership) of IEI expressing their desire to open a Students’ Chapter at the Engineering College/ Polytechnic mentioning the branches of Engineering.
In a College/ University/ Institution, at least 50 numbers of students (in Electronics & Telecommunication and Computer Engineering branches) irrespective of the year is required for opening a Students’ Chapter.
In a College/ University/ Institution, at least 30 numbers of students (other than Electronics & Telecommunication and Computer Engineering branches) irrespective of the year is required for opening a Students’ Chapter.
To enable formation of a Chapter in any recognized Polytechnic, minimum number of member required is 50. There shall be only one Chapter in a polytechnic.
This strength of membership shall be mandatory for opening as also for continuing a Students Chapter. However, to motivate all the Students to enrol themselves in the chapter.
Guidelines of Opening of New Students’ Chapter/ Renewal of Existing Students’ Chapter at Engineering Colleges/ Polytechnics
Download
Fees
i. For Degree Engineering College:
Membership fee for Student Chapter	Subscription (₹) [incl. GST]	Share of College/Institution (₹)	Share of IEI HQ (₹) [incl. GST]
First Year	644	360	284
Second Year
Third Year
Fourth Year
ii. For Polytechnic:
Membership fee for Student Chapter	Subscription (₹) [incl. GST]	Share of College/Institution (₹)	Share of IEI HQ (₹) [incl. GST]
First Year	536	300	236
Second Year
Third Year
Note: Payment should be made by multi‑city Cheque / Demand Draft in favour of “The Institution of Engineers (India)”, payable at Kolkata.

LOGIN
Pull to refresh
Student Chapter
Overview
Students’ Chapters of IEI in Engineering Colleges or Polytechnic may be established as per Rules and Regulations of IEI.
The Student Members (SMIE) of IEI shall be Member of Students' Chapters.
Benefits of Students’ Chapters
Unlock endless opportunities for learning, networking, and career growth for Students.
Participate in Technical Events
Seminars, Workshops, and National Conventions etc. organized by IEI State/Local Centres.
Hosting Technical Events
Students can organize various technical programm, Paper Presentation, Model Presentation, Start up Programm etc.
Library Access
Enjoy unlimited access to the IEI State/Local Centre libraries for research and study.
Networking & Mentorship
Connect with IEI members and industry professionals for career guidance.
Exclusive Membership Benefits
Eligible students can become Corporate Member of IEI after completion of graduation.
Scholarships & Awards
Top-performing students’ chapters receive cash prizes.
Students’ Chapter Newsletter
Stay updated with the latest news and developments through the exclusive newsletter.
Publish Research Papers
Students can publish research articles in Students’ Journal released every December.
How to Open Students' Chapters
Initial request from an Engineering College/ Polytechnic to be made to the Deputy Director (Membership) of IEI expressing their desire to open a Students’ Chapter at the Engineering College/ Polytechnic mentioning the branches of Engineering.
In a College/ University/ Institution, at least 50 numbers of students (in Electronics & Telecommunication and Computer Engineering branches) irrespective of the year is required for opening a Students’ Chapter.
In a College/ University/ Institution, at least 30 numbers of students (other than Electronics & Telecommunication and Computer Engineering branches) irrespective of the year is required for opening a Students’ Chapter.
To enable formation of a Chapter in any recognized Polytechnic, minimum number of member required is 50. There shall be only one Chapter in a polytechnic.
This strength of membership shall be mandatory for opening as also for continuing a Students Chapter. However, to motivate all the Students to enrol themselves in the chapter.
Guidelines of Opening of New Students’ Chapter/ Renewal of Existing Students’ Chapter at Engineering Colleges/ Polytechnics

FAQ
Membership
1. What are the Classes of Membership?
Corporate
Fellow – FIE
Member – MIE
Associate Member – AMIE
Non-Corporate
Student Member – SMIE
Member Technologist – MTIE
Associate Member Technologist – AMTIE
Senior Technician – ST
Institutional Member – IM
2. What are the Qualifications for Membership?
Qualification for Membership as described in the Bye-Laws and Regulations of the Council is applicable for every candidates for election as member of any class.
3. Give me an Abridged Eligibility Guidelines for the Corporate Membership.
Click here to see the details of Abridged Eligibility Guidelines for the Corporate Membership.
4. What are the Privileges of Corporate Members?
Privileges of Corporate Members :
Entitlement to have ‘Chartered Engineer’ certificate on payment of requisite fee.
Entitlement to receive IEI’s journals, technical monographs, papers, conference proceedings.
Entitlement to receive copies of IEI's News and Technorama free of cost.
Access to the Engineering Information Service Centre (EISC) at the Headquarters as well as at the state and local centres.
Participation in continuing education programme at the Engineering Staff College of India (ESCI), Hyderabad and at state and local.
Participation in the numerous seminars, symposia, conventions, workshops, lectures, conferences, congresses and other events held at national, regional and local levels.
Participation in international conferences.
Entitlement to enjoy facilities and benefits from 27 foreign professional bodies with whom IEI has bilateral relationships.
Opportunity to act as arbitrators in arbitration matters relating to engineering jobs and services.
Sharing ideas, know-how and experience with fellow members by publishing articles in IEI’s journals.
Entitlement to reserve and stay in retiring rooms available at the Headquarters and at Centres at concessional rates.
A Corporate Member receives a Letter of election. All the above privileges given to him are stated in this letter.
5. How do I become a member?
Application forms for Corporate Membership FIE/MIE/AMIE are available at IEI State and Local Centre. Forms can also be downloaded from the website. Hard copy of the application form duly filled in along with the requisite documents duly attested by FIE/MIE/AMIE as specified in the form must be sent to the Headquarters. The application form must be signed by the supporter(s), who is a member of the IEI in the Category of FIE/MIE/AMIE, quoting the valid membership number. All the copies of documents accompanying the membership form must be attested by one of the supporters who has signed the membership form. Remittance should be made by Demand Draft (DD) in favour of ‘The Institution of Engineers (India)’, payable at Kolkata. The draft should be sent along with the membership application form addressed to The Director (Membership), The Institution of Engineers (India), 8 Gokhale Road, Kolkata 700020, superscribing on the top of the envelope ‘Membership Application Form’.
Apply Online
6. Time required to process application?
Acknowledgement is sent by SMS regarding receipt of money within seven working days after receiving the documents. The SMS massage containing the reference no. should be noted for any future communication. The processing of application for enrollment as corporate member normally takes two months time and that of non corporate ST members takes three months time at present from the date of acknowledgement. In case of non-receipt of SMS, please use our IVRS No. (033)40155400 to ascertain receipt of money by giving the six-digit DD number. This will also prompt the 12 digit Ref No. which is unique number to identify every application. For any future communication with the headquarters till the enrolment and to know about the status through IVRS, this 12 digit reference number should be quoted/used.
7. What are the Important points to remember?
Please do not forget to attest all the document
...[truncated]

The Institution of Engineers (India)
Our Bye-Laws and Regulations outline the core principles that guide our organization. They ensure transparency, accountability, and professionalism in all our operations. Adherence to these guidelines helps us maintain the highest standards of integrity, ethical behavior, and organizational excellence.
Bye-Laws
Bye-Laws are the rules of IEI to regulates its own affairs e.g. governances , rights and privileges of members, Technical activities . Any changes in the Bye-Laws are required to be approved by the Corporate Members at the Extraordinary General Meeting.
Bye-Laws
Download
Regulations
Regulations are the rules which regulates the functions and activities of the centres of IEI. Any changes in the Regulations are required to be approved by the Corporate Members at the Special General Meeting.
Regulations
Download

IEI Fora and Organ
The Institution of Engineers (India) (IEI), in line with its Royal Charter principles, has established Autonomous Bodies in the form of Fora & Organs—pioneering platforms dedicated to innovation, research, societal development, and policy advocacy. These initiatives empower engineers to drive sustainable development, shaping a stronger, technologically advanced India.

PAGE : Publication - Books
URL  : https://www.ieindia.org/web/publication#books
TITLE: IEI
STATUS: ok | HTTP 200
----------------------------------------------------------------------
CONTENT:
Contact Us
LOGIN
Pull to refresh
IEI Publications
Overview
IEI is instrumental in publishing journals, books, Annual Technical Volumes, Compendium on R & D Projects, Annual Reports, Proceedings of Indian Engineering Congress, National Conventions, and International Conferences.
IEI Springer Journals
To augment the quality of the Journals, in a landmark achievement, the Institution has signed the co-publishing agreement with M/s Springer (India) Pvt Ltd, New Delhi, on 10th August 2011 at Headquarters in Kolkata. Both IE(I) and Springer have agreed for the common cause of improvement in the quality of journals, impact factor, citation index and also to bring the Journals within the reach of one and all in all corners of the globe.
All 15 engineering divisional journals have been grouped into five series –Series A, Series B, Series C, Series D & Series E.
SERIES-A
SERIES-B
SERIES-C
SERIES-D
SERIES-E
JOURNAL OF THE INSTITUTION OF ENGINEERS: SERIES A
Areas Covered:
Civil Engineering
Architectural Engineering
Environmental Engineering
Agricultural Engineering
Series A serves the national and international engineering community through dissemination of scientific knowledge on practical engineering and design methodologies pertaining to Civil, Architectural, Environmental and Agricultural engineering. Original manuscripts are published through Double-Blind Peer Review in all the areas including (but not limited to) structural designs, green buildings, environmental pollutions or agricultural machinery / techniques related researches. It covers all possible areas of latest research and developmental works in the field of infrastructure developments, waste management techniques, harvestings methodologies, rainwater harvestings etc. so that the researchers, scientists or professionals can easily motivate themselves to pursue the work.
Months of Publication:
March
June
September
December
View Journal
Submit Paper
Know More

IEI Publications
Overview
IEI is instrumental in publishing journals, books, Annual Technical Volumes, Compendium on R & D Projects, Annual Reports, Proceedings of Indian Engineering Congress, National Conventions, and International Conferences.
IEI Springer Journals
To augment the quality of the Journals, in a landmark achievement, the Institution has signed the co-publishing agreement with M/s Springer (India) Pvt Ltd, New Delhi, on 10th August 2011 at Headquarters in Kolkata. Both IE(I) and Springer have agreed for the common cause of improvement in the quality of journals, impact factor, citation index and also to bring the Journals within the reach of one and all in all corners of the globe.
All 15 engineering divisional journals have been grouped into five series –Series A, Series B, Series C, Series D & Series E.
SERIES-A
SERIES-B
SERIES-C
SERIES-D
SERIES-E
JOURNAL OF THE INSTITUTION OF ENGINEERS: SERIES A
Areas Covered:
Civil Engineering
Architectural Engineering
Environmental Engineering
Agricultural Engineering
Series A serves the national and international engineering community through dissemination of scientific knowledge on practical engineering and design methodologies pertaining to Civil, Architectural, Environmental and Agricultural engineering. Original manuscripts are published through Double-Blind Peer Review in all the areas including (but not limited to) structural designs, green buildings, environmental pollutions or agricultural machinery / techniques related researches. It covers all possible areas of latest research and developmental works in the field of infrastructure developments, waste management techniques, harvestings methodologies, rainwater harvestings etc. so that the researchers, scientists or professionals can easily motivate themselves to pursue the work.
Months of Publication:
March
June
September
December

PAGE : Certification - Int PE (alt path)

TITLE: International Professional Engineering - The Institution of Engineers (India) - IEI Official Website
STATUS: ok | HTTP 200
----------------------------------------------------------------------
CONTENT:
Contact Us
LOGIN
Pull to refresh
About
By virtue of being a full member of The International Professional Engineers Agreement (IPEA) since 2009, The Institution of Engineers (India) represents India and have been empowered to establish and maintain the India section of the International Professional Engineers (IntPE) Register .
The International Professional Engineers Agreement (IPEA) (previously known as the Engineers Mobility Forum (EMF)), is a multi-national agreement between engineering organisations in the member jurisdictions which creates the framework for the establishment of an international standard of competence for professional engineering, The International Professional Engineers (India) registered with IEI, may receive credit when seeking registration or licensure in the jurisdiction of another member , i.e this will facilitate an engineer in mobility across member jurisdictions.
In furtherance of these functions of the profession, it will be aimed that only a Professional Engineer, either working individually or in an organizational set-up will approve designs/drawings/reports/products before these are released for use by the public at large. Such certified professional engineers will be designated as Professional Engineer (PE).
Expected Benefit OF IntPE / Expected Outcomes of IntPE
Gives confidence to employer/prospective employer about competency of Engineer in a particular domain
Enhances an engineering professional’s stature
Makes them suitable for higher levels of responsibility
In future, only a professional engineer may prepare, sign, seal and submit engineering plans and drawings to a public authority for approval, or to seal engineering work for public and private clients
With the growing economy and massive expansion of technological infrastructure, the market demand of IntPE certified engineers are expected to be much higher
Int.P.Eng. (India) Certification enables an engineer to become an independent engineering consultant, a valuer, a planner, a designer, an educator.
The International Professional Engineers, registered with IEI, may receive credit when seeking registration or licensure in the jurisdiction of another member i.e this will facilitate an engineer in mobility across member jurisdictions.
Other member jurisdictions of the IPEA agreement
Australia - Represented by Engineers Australia (EA) (1997)
Canada - Represented by Engineers Canada (EC) (1997)
Chinese Taipei - Represented by Chinese Institute of Engineers (CIE) (2009)
Ireland - Represented by Engineers Ireland (EI) (1997)
Hong Kong China - Represented by Hong Kong Institution of Engineers (HKIE) (1997)
India - Represented by Institution of Engineers India (IEI) (2009)
Japan - Represented by Institution of Professional Engineers Japan (IPEJ) (1999)
Korea - Represented by Korean Professional Engineers Association (KPEA) (2000)
Malaysia - Represented by Institution of Engineers Malaysia (IEM) (1999)
New Zealand - Represented by Engineering New Zealand (EngNZ) (1997)
Singapore - Represented by Institution of Engineers Singapore (IES) (2007)
South Africa - Represented by Engineering Council South Africa (ECSA) (2007)
Sri Lanka - Represented by Institution of Engineers Sri Lanka (IESL) (2007)
United Kingdom - Represented by Engineering Council United Kingdom (ECUK) (1997)
United States - Represented by National Council of Examiners for Engineering and Surveying (NCEES) (1997)
Provisional Members
Bangladesh - Represented by Bangladesh Professional Engineers Registration Board (BPERB)
Pakistan - Represented by Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC)
Russia - Represented by Association for Engineering Education Russia (AEER)
Holland - Represented by Koninklijk Instituut Van Ingenieurs (KIVI)
However, for the IntPE certified engineers to enjoy the benefit of mobility and recognition in the member economy country IEI needs to have mobility agreement with each of the member economy country. As of date there is no bilateral agreement of IEI with any of

Awards and Recognitions
Overview
IEI recognizes the professional excellence of practising engineers, best papers published in IEI Journals, highlights the performance of industry Leaders and academic institutions for nation building.
Industry Excellence Award
The benchmarks created by the industries in India have included productivity, quality, safety and performance assurance thereby giving India the rightful place in the global markets. Realizing that such industries can provide the leadership to a large number of other industries in the country, IEI instituted the IEI Industry Excellence Awards in the year 2008, so as to recognize industry leaders for their innovation, excellence in engineering operations and thereby enable them to lead their industry in a competitive manner. Industries, namely, Tata Consultancy Services, Steel Authority of India Limited, Tata Motors Limited, Larsen & Toubro Limited, Neyveli Lignite Corporation Limited, Bharat Heavy Electricals Limited, National Thermal Power Corporation Limited, Hindustan Aeronautics Limited, J K Tyre and Industries Limited, MECON Limited, NBCC (India) Limited, Goa Shipyard Ltd. are amongst the recipients of the Award.
List Of Recipients
Nomination Form IEA 2026
IEA Brochure 2026
Engineering Education Excellence Award
The IEI Engineering Education Excellence Award has been instituted to recognize leading Engineering Educational Institutions and encourage for better and effective engineering education across the country. Significant development has taken place in the engineering education sector which has created benchmarks for the others to follow. The universities and institutions are no more confined to pedagogy but also diversified to R&D activities , Consultancy, Patents, Publication, Skill Development Programs, Industry interface and introduction of New Education Policy (NEP), thereby giving India the rightful place globally. Realizing that such institution can provide the leadership to a large number of others in the country, it has been considered appropriate by the IEI Council to institute the IEI Engineering Education Excellence Awards.
List Of Recipients
Nomination Form EEEA 2026
EEEA Brochure 2026
IEI Young Engineers Award
With a view to promote the pursuit of excellence in the field of engineering, IEI has instituted 'IEI Young Engineers Award'. The Award consists of a Plaque and a Certificate. The purpose of the Award is to recognize outstanding achievements/contributions made by young engineers in engineering research, excellence in engineering technology development, technology transfer, etc. Any engineer citizen of India not older than 35 years of age/ women engineer citizen not older than 37 years of age as on March 31, 2025 is eligible for the Award, provided that he/she is a Corporate Member of IEI or has applied for IEI Membership. The IEI Young Engineers Award is presented to awardees for all the 15 Engineering Divisions of the IEI during the respective National Conventions.
The awardees attending the National Convention will be provided with free accommodation & their traveling expenses (AC-3 Tier train fare by shortest route) will be reimbursed on production of original documents.
Recipients Of IEI Young Engineers Award
Notification for YEA 2026
YEA Application Form 2026
Prize for Best Papers published in IEI Springer Journals
The Institution gives away a large number of prizes, awards and certificates to the authors of the papers of high technical standard published in the IEI-Springer Journals of all Divisions and thereby extending recognition to individual achievements and activities in advancing the science and the art of engineering.
Best Journal Paper Prizes
